<div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">REPORT OF INDEPENDENT REGISTERED
PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM</font></u></b><a name="ReportOfIndependentRegisteredPubl_113300"></a></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To
Participants and Administrative Committee of</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Kroger Co. 401(k)&nbsp;Retirement Savings Account Plan:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We have audited the accompanying statements of net assets available for
benefits of The Kroger Co. 401(k)&nbsp;Retirement Savings Account Plan as of December&nbsp;31,
2009 and 2008, and the related statements of changes in net assets available
for benefits for the years then ended.&#160;
These financial statements are the responsibility of the Plan&#146;s
management.&#160; Our responsibility is to
express an opinion on these financial statements based on our audits.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We conducted our audits in accordance with standards of the Public
Company Accounting Oversight Board (United States).&#160; Those standards require that we plan and
perform the audit to obtain reasonable assurance about whether the financial
statements are free of material misstatement.&#160;
An audit includes examining, on a test basis, evidence supporting the
amounts and disclosures in the financial statements.&#160; An audit also includes assessing the
accounting principles used and significant estimates made by management, as
well as evaluating the overall financial statement presentation.&#160; We believe that our audits provide a
reasonable basis for our opinion.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In our opinion, the financial statements referred to above present
fairly, in all material respects, the net assets available for benefits of the
Plan as of December&nbsp;31, 2009 and 2008, and the changes in its net assets
available for benefits for the years then ended in conformity with accounting
principles generally accepted in the United States of America.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our
audit was conducted for the purpose of forming an opinion on the basic
financial statements taken as a whole.&#160;
The accompanying supplemental Schedule of Assets (Held at End of Year)
and Schedule of Reportable Transactions are presented for the purpose of
additional analysis and are not a required part of the basic financial
statements but are supplementary information required by the Department of
Labor Rules&nbsp;and Regulations for Reporting and Disclosure under the
Employee Retirement Income Security Act of 1974.&#160; The supplemental schedules are the
responsibility of the Plan&#146;s management.&#160;
The supplemental schedules have been subjected to the auditing
procedures applied in our audit of the basic financial statements and, in our
opinion, are fairly stated in all material respects in relation to the basic
financial statements taken as a whole.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">/s/
Clark, Schaefer, Hackett&nbsp;&amp; Co.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Cincinnati,
Ohio</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">June&nbsp;28,
2010</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table
of Contents</a></font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">THE KROGER
CO. 401(K)&nbsp;RETIREMENT SAVINGS ACCOUNT PLAN</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Notes to Financial
Statements<a name="NotesToFinancialStatements_113330"></a></font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.75pt;text-indent:-18.75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Description of Plan</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.75pt;text-indent:-18.75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following description of The Kroger Co. 401(k)&nbsp;Retirement
Savings Account Plan (Plan) provides only general information.&#160; Participants should refer to the plan
document for a more complete description of Plan provisions.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">General</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Plan, which began January&nbsp;1, 2007, is sponsored by The Kroger Co., an Ohio
corporation, and its wholly-owned subsidiaries (collectively the Company).&#160; The Plan is a defined contribution plan
covering all employees of the Company who have attained age 21, have been
employed 30 days, and have completed 72 hours of service within the 30-day
period, excluding those employees eligible to participate under another defined
contribution pension plan or defined benefit pension plan sponsored by the
Company.&#160; It is subject to the provisions
of the Employee Retirement Income Security Act of 1974, as amended (ERISA).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Contributions</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:.5in;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Employee</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Subject
to certain limits, participants may contribute up to 75% of compensation per
pay period to the Plan.&#160; It is at the
discretion of participants to modify and direct investments.&#160; Participants are eligible to make catch-up
contributions beginning in the year in which they reach age 50.&#160; Participants are also permitted to deposit
into the Plan distributions from other qualified plans.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:.5in;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Employer</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
employer will credit the participant&#146;s account with a match and/or an automatic
contribution if the participant meets the eligibility requirements.&#160; The matching contribution is 100% of the
first 3% of the participant&#146;s plan compensation contributed as a salary
redirection contribution, plus 50% of the next 2% of the participant&#146;s plan
compensation contributed as a salary redirection contribution.&#160; At the end of each plan year, the employer
will, if necessary, make a &#147;true-up&#148; matching contribution in the first quarter
of the following year.&#160; Subject to
certain limits, the Company also pays an automatic contribution of 1% or 2%
based on the participant&#146;s years of vesting service.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Participant Accounts</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Each
participant account is credited with the participant contribution, matching
contribution (if any), automatic contribution, and an allocation of Plan
earnings or losses.&#160; Allocations of
earnings or losses are based upon the performance of the </font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4<a name="PB_4_101819_5796"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='4',FILE='C:\JMS\105588\10-13252-3\task4169309\13252-3-ba.htm',USER='105588',CD='Jun 29 13:40 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">investment
funds chosen by the participant.&#160; The
benefit to which a participant is entitled is the benefit that can be provided
from the participant&#146;s vested account.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Vesting</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">All
employee contributions, employer matching contributions, transferred accounts,
and rollover accounts are fully vested at all times.&#160; The participant&#146;s vested interest in all
automatic contributions, if any, will be determined based upon the participant&#146;s
years of vesting service with the employer.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Benefits</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Payment
of benefits can be made under various methods, depending upon the reason for
the distribution, such as termination of service, death, or retirement, as well
as other factors.&#160; At termination, those
participants with a balance of less than or equal to $1,000 will receive a
single lump sum distribution.&#160; Absent specific
elections by the participant, those with balances greater than $1,000 and less
than or equal to $5,000 shall be distributed, in the form of a direct rollover,
to an individual retirement account designated by the Plan Administrator.&#160; Those with balances greater than $5,000 may
elect to leave their funds in the Plan or choose other options.&#160; Participants are entitled to benefits
beginning at normal retirement age (generally age 65).&#160; Benefits are recorded when paid.&#160; Unclaimed benefits are forfeited and are
applied to pay Plan expenses.&#160; Forfeited
unclaimed benefits are restored if a participant later establishes a valid
benefit claim.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Participant Loans</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Plan permits participants to borrow from their vested account less all vested
automatic contributions.&#160; The maximum
amount that may be borrowed is the lesser of $50,000 or 50% of the vested
balance of the account.&#160; Loan terms range
from 1 - 4 years or up to 6 years for the purchase of a primary residence.&#160; The loans are collateralized by the balance
in the participant&#146;s account and bear interest at a rate of Prime plus 1.0%.&#160; The rate is changed quarterly and the Prime
rate used for a quarter is the Prime rate on the last business day of the
previous quarter.&#160; Principal and interest
are paid through periodic payroll deductions.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Reclassification</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Certain
prior year amounts have been reclassified to conform to the current year
presentation.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Summary of
Significant Accounting Policies</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Basis of accounting</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The financial statements of
the Plan are prepared using the accrual basis of accounting in conformity with
accounting principles generally accepted in the United States of America.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5<a name="PB_5_101837_2897"></a></font></p>

<div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Master Trust</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The investments of the Plan,
along with investments of other plans of The Kroger Co. and its subsidiaries,
are located for investment purposes in a master trust pursuant to an agreement
dated July&nbsp;1, 2004 (the Master Trust), between Bank of America N.A., as
successor in interest to Merrill Lynch&nbsp;&amp; Co., FSB, the trustee, and
the Company.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Investment valuation and income recognition</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Plan&#146;s investments within the Master Trust are stated at fair value.&#160; Fair value is the price that would be
received to sell an asset or paid to transfer a liability in an orderly
transaction between market participants at the measurement date.&#160; See Note 8 for discussion of fair value
measurements.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Purchases
and sales of securities are recorded on a trade date basis.&#160; Gains or losses on sales of securities are
based on average cost.&#160; Dividends are
recorded on the ex-dividend date.&#160; Income
from other investments is recorded as earned.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Investment
contracts held by a defined contribution plan are required to be reported at
fair value.&#160; However, contract value is the
relevant measurement attribute for that portion of the net assets available for
benefits of a defined contribution plan attributable to fully
benefit-responsive investment contracts because contract value is the amount
participants would receive if they were to initiate a permitted transaction
under the terms of the Plan.&#160; The Plan
invests in investment contracts through The Kroger Defined Contribution Plan
Master Trust.&#160; The Statement of Net
Assets Available for Benefits presents the fair value of the investment in the
Master Trust as well as the adjustment of the investment in the Master Trust
from fair value to contract value relating to investment contracts.&#160; The Statement of Changes in Net Assets
Available for Benefits is prepared on a contract value basis.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Estimates</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
presentation of financial statements in conformity with accounting principles
generally accepted in the United States requires management to make estimates
and assumptions that affect certain reported amounts and disclosures.&#160; Actual results may differ from those
estimates.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Administrative expenses</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan will pay the
administrative costs and expenses of the Plan, including the trustee and
management fees.&#160; Any expenses that are
unable to be allocated to participants are paid by the Company.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Subsequent events</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company evaluates events
and transactions occurring subsequent to the date of the financial statements
for matters requiring recognition or disclosure in the financial statements.
The accompanying financial statements consider events through the date on which
the financial statements were available to be issued.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6<a name="PB_6_101853_3020"></a></font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of
Contents</a></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Transfers</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During
2009 and 2008, participant balances of approximately $6,000 and $(27,000),
respectively, were transferred from (to) The Kroger Co. Savings Plan.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Investments</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Plan provides for participant directed investments into common stock of The
Kroger Co., mutual funds, collective trusts, stable value funds, and certain
retirement date funds, through the investment in the Master Trust.&#160; Investments that represent 5% or more of the
Plan&#146;s net assets as of December&nbsp;31, 2009 and 2008 are as follows (in
thousands):</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Included
in investment income from the Plan&#146;s participation in the Master Trust is
appreciation (depreciation) from investments bought sold and held during the
year of $182,841 and $(301,913) for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2009 and
2008, respectively.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Nonparticipant-Directed
Investments</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Investments
in The Kroger Co. common stock within the Master Trust are generated from
participant-directed contributions and Company matching contributions. Employee
and employer amounts invested in The Kroger Co. common stock cannot be
separately determined, but can be invested in other investment option at any
time at the election of the employee. Investments in The Kroger Co. common
stock are considered nonparticipant-directed for disclosure purposes.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Investment Contracts</u>:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Master Trust holds several synthetic investment contracts which are
managed by investment fund managers.&#160; The
Master Trust also purchases wrapper contracts from financial institutions which
provide assurance that crediting rates will never be less than zero.&#160; All Plans have an undivided interest in each
investment contract.&#160; The investment
contracts are fully benefit-responsive.&#160;
A fully benefit-responsive investment provides a liquidity guarantee by
a financially responsible third party of principal and previously accrued
interest for liquidations, transfers, loans, or withdrawals initiated by Plan
participants under the terms of the ongoing Plan.&#160; Certain employer-initiated events (i.e.
layoffs, mergers, bankruptcy, Plan termination) are not eligible for the
liquidity guarantee.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In general, issuers may terminate the investment contracts and settle
at other than contract value if the qualification status of the employer or
plan changes, breach of material obligations under the contract or misrepresentation
by the contract holder, or failure of the underlying portfolio to conform to
the pre-established investment guidelines.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan Administrator does not believe that the occurrence of any such
event, which would limit the Plan&#146;s ability to transact at contract value with
participants, is probable.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following information relates to the Master Trust interest in
investment contracts (in thousands):</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
crediting interest rate range for the investment contracts is based upon the
contract rate or a predetermined formula that factors in duration, market
value, and book value of the investment.&#160;
Certain of the crediting rates are adjusted quarterly.&#160; The minimum crediting interest rate for these
investments is zero.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">653,412</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net
investment income (loss) of the Master Trust for the year ended December&nbsp;31,
2009 and 2008 was $178,690 and $(597,682), respectively.&#160; Included in these amounts are dividends of
$59,016 and $74,594 at December&nbsp;31, 2009 and 2008, respectively.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
underlying investments within the synthetic contracts include corporate,
government and mortgage backed debt securities.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As
of December&nbsp;31, 2009 and 2008, the Plan&#146;s interest in the net assets of
the Master Trust was 34.67% and 23.70%, respectively.&#160; The Master Trust allocates individual assets
to each plan participating in the Master Trust arrangement.&#160; Therefore, the investment results of the Plan
may not reflect its proportionate interest in the Master Trust.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Fair Value Measurements</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:.3pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
financial statement elements currently required to be measured at fair value,
Generally Accepted Accounting Principles define fair value and establish a
framework for measuring fair value and disclosing the fair value measurements
utilized. The standards define fair value as the price that would be received
to sell an asset or paid to transfer a liability (exit price) regardless of
whether an observable liquid market price exists.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Generally
Accepted Accounting Principles establish a fair value hierarchy that
categorizes the inputs to valuation techniques that are used to measure fair
value into three levels:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Level 1 includes observable inputs which
reflect quoted prices for identical assets or liabilities in active markets at
the measurement date.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9<a name="PB_9_104316_7056"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Level 2 includes observable inputs for
assets or liabilities other than quoted prices included in Level 1 and it
includes valuation techniques which use prices for similar assets and
liabilities.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Level 3 includes
unobservable inputs which reflect the reporting entity&#146;s estimates of the
assumptions that market participants would use in pricing the asset or
liability, including assumptions about risk.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
asset&#146;s fair value measurement level within the fair value hierarchy is based
on the lowest level of any input that is significant to the fair value
measurement. Valuation techniques used need to maximize the use of observable
inputs and minimize the use of unobservable inputs.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
following is a description of the valuation methods used for assets measured at
fair value. There have been no changes in methodologies used at
December&nbsp;31, 2009 and 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Cash
and cash equivalents: The carrying value approximates fair value.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Common
Stocks: The fair values of these securities are based on observable
market quotations for identical assets and are valued at the closing price
reported on the active market on which the individual securities are traded.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Mutual
Funds: The fair values of these securities are primarily based on
observable market quotations for identical assets and are valued at the closing
price reported on the active market on which the individual securities are
traded.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Guaranteed
Investment Contracts: The investments include cash and cash equivalents, fixed
maturity guaranteed investment contracts (GICs) and constant duration GICs. The
fair value of the investments are calculated using the present value of the
contract&#146;s future cash flow values discounted by comparable duration Wall
Street Journal GIC Index rates. Fair values for variable synthetic GICs are
calculated using the present value of the contract&#146;s future cash flow values
discounted by comparable swap rates. Fair values for constant duration
synthetic GICs are calculated using the market values provided by the external
investment managers.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Collective
Trusts: The collective trust funds are public investment vehicles valued using
a Net Asset Value (NAV) provided by the manager of each fund.&#160; The NAV is based on the underlying net assets
owned by the fund, divided by the number of shares outstanding.&#160; The NAV&#146;s unit price is quoted on a private
market that is not active.&#160; However, the
NAV is based on the fair value of the underlying securities within the fund,
which are traded on an active market, and valued at the closing price reported
on the active market on which those individual securities are traded. The
significant investment strategies of the funds are as described in the
financial statements provided by each fund.&#160;
There are no restrictions on redemptions from these funds.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Retirement
Date Funds: Retirement date funds are made up of investments in mutual
funds, custom funds, and collective trusts, and are valued in a manner
consistent with that described above for Mutual Funds and the Interest in
Master Trust. </font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10<a name="PB_10_104715_5335"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Participant
Loans: Participant loans are valued at their outstanding amortized
balances, which approximate fair value.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
methods described above may produce a fair value calculation that may not be
indicative of net realizable value or reflective of future fair values.
Furthermore, while the Plan believes its valuations methods are appropriate and
consistent with other market participants, the use of different methodologies
or assumptions to determine the fair value of certain financial instruments
could result in a different fair value measurement.&#160; Investment securities, in general, are
exposed to various risks, such as interest rate, credit and overall market
volatility.&#160; Due to the level of risk
associated with certain investment securities, it is reasonably possible that
changes in the fair values of investment securities will occur in the near term
and, that such changes could materially affect the amounts reported in the
statements of net assets available for benefits.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">While
all the investments of the participating plans are deemed part of the Master
Trust, each plan does maintain a separate accounting of its share of the
investments in the Master Trust, which is reflected below.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
following table sets forth by level, within the fair value hierarchy, the Plan&#146;s
assets at fair value as of December&nbsp;31, 2009:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="border-collapse:collapse;width:100.0%;">
 <tr>
  <td width="29%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:29.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.5%;">
  <p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
  </td>
  <td width="67%" colspan="11" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:67.5%;">
  <p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:8.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(in thousands)</font></b></p>
  </td>
  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.0%;">
  <p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
  </td>

 <tr>
  <td width="29%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:29.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.5%;">
  <p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Income Tax
Status</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan does not currently
have a determination letter from the Internal Revenue Service.&#160; The EIN for the Plan ends in &#147;0&#148;.&#160; Therefore the plan is on cycle E in regards
to applying for a determination letter from the Internal Revenue Service.&#160; Thus, the application cannot be sent until
2/1/2010 at the earliest and 1/31/2011 at the latest.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10. &#160;&#160;<u>Plan Termination</u>:</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Although it has not expressed any intent to do so, the Company has the
right under the Plan to terminate the Plan at any time subject to the
provisions of ERISA.&#160; In the event of any
total or partial termination or discontinuance, the accounts of all affected
participants shall remain fully vested and non-forfeitable.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11.&#160; <u>Related-party and
Party-in-interest Transactions (in thousands)</u>:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan&#146;s portion of its interest in the Master Trust included
$111,874 and $133,798 of The Kroger Co. common shares at December&nbsp;31, 2009
and 2008, respectively, at fair value.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:.3pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Plan purchased 2,589 and 3,401 shares of The Kroger Co. common shares at a cost
of&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; $56,756 and $90,519 in 2009 and
2008, respectively, through its interest in the Master Trust.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:.3pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Plan sold 2,175 and 3,296 shares of The Kroger Co. common shares for $47,803
and $89,253 with a realized loss of $(451) and a realized gain of $6,049 in
2009 and 2008, respectively, through its interest in the Master Trust.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:.3pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Bank
of America, N.A. and Merrill Lynch provide recordkeeping and investment management
services to the Plan.&#160; Therefore,
transactions with Bank of America, N.A. and Merrill Lynch qualify as
party-in-interest transactions.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">12.&#160; <u>Reconciliation of Financial Statements to Form&nbsp;5500</u>:</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net investment gain (loss)
from master trust investment accounts on the Form&nbsp;5500 will also reflect
these adjustments.</font></p>

INDEPENDENT REGISTERED PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM</font></b></p>

the Plan Administrator of</font></p>

consent to incorporation by reference in the Registration Statement (No.&nbsp;333-138152)

Co. 401(k)&nbsp;Retirement Savings Account Plan as of December&nbsp;31, 2009 and 2008, and the related statements of
changes in net assets available for benefits and the supplemental schedules for
the years then ended, which report appears in the December&nbsp;31, 2009 annual report on Form&nbsp;11-K of The
Kroger Co. 401(k)&nbsp;Retirement Savings Account Plan.</font></p>
